completion and assurance 51 completion of improvements required prior to final plat approval the applicant will complete and dedicate all public improvements prior to final plat approval 52 performance agreement and letter of credit notwithstanding the requirement of above in the alternative the planning commission may approve a final plat and allow the recording of the same provided that the applicant first delivers to the city a performance agreement in such form and substance as approved by the city attorney and a letter of credit securing the applicants obligations to construct and dedicate all public improvements required by the planning commission in no event shall the plat be recorded prior to the delivery to the city of the executed performance agreement and issued letter of credit the performance agreement and letter of credit shall provide for an annual ten percent 10% escalator that automatically becomes effective on each anniversary of the issuance of the letter of credit the performance agreement and letter of credit will comply with these subdivision regulations and will be satisfactory to the city attorney as to form sufficiency and manner of execution the amount of the letter of credit will be established by the planning commission in consultation with the city engineer and will be in an amount sufficient to secure the satisfactory construction installation and dedication of the required improvements a the performance agreement the performance agreement will stipulate the work to be performed by general categories and the estimated value or cost of each category the performance agreement will also stipulate a completion date for all of the work to be performed the performance agreement will only be entered into by owner of the property b the letter of credit the letter of credit will be an irrevocable standby letter of credit issued by or confirmed by a financial institution located in davidson county tennessee or an adjoining county the term of the letter of credit will be co 21 adopted  terminus with the term set forth in the performance agreement  however in no event shall the letter of credit terminate prior to the proper completion of the improvements secured by the letter of credit and the inspection and approval of same as shall be evidenced in writing and signed by the city manager and city engineer c governmental agencies governmental agencies to which these contract provisions and security instruments apply may file in lieu of said contract or security instrument a letter from an agent authorized to act on their behalf agreeing to comply with the provisions of this temporary improvements when applicable the applicant will build and pay for all costs of temporary improvements required by the planning commission and will maintain such for the period specified by the planning commission prior to construction of any temporary facility or improvement a letter of credit will be issued which will insure that the temporary facilities will be properly constructed maintained and removed 54 costs of improvements all required improvements will be made by the applicant at the applicants expense any provisions for reimbursement by the city or any utility district will be by separate agreement with the applicable governmental entity 55 improvement failure upon inspection if the city manager or designee of the city manager finds that any of the required improvements have not been constructed in accordance with the applicable city construction standards and specifications or in compliance with the approved plans andor the terms of the performance agreement then the applicant will be responsible for correcting the default or deficiency and for completing the improvements to the required standards the applicant shall also be responsible for the citys administrative costs and other professionals expenses incurred in connection with the incomplete deficient or defective work whenever the cost to complete improvements is secured by a letter of credit or other instrument the funds available pursuant to same may be used to correct any defect or deficiency andor to complete the improvements according to plans and specifications if the remedial work will not be properly completed within ten 10 days of the discovery of same then the applicant shall increase the amount of the then effective letter of credit by the cost of the remedial work to be approved by the city manager and city engineer plus fifteen percent 15% 56 release reduction or extension a satisfactory completion the city manager will not release nor reduce a letter of credit or other security instrument acceptable the city until all required improvements have been completed inspected and approved by the city engineer and all associated andor surplus construction materials are removed from the site there will be no reduction or release said security instrument if there are any outstanding administrative penalties or violations related to the property which may be satisfied by payment under the letter of credit or other security instrument b reduction of letter of credit the board of commissioners may reduce the amount of a letter of credit or other security instrument upon the recommendation by 22 adopted  the city manager and city engineer following the applicants demonstration of satisfactory completion of the public improvements or portions thereof such reductions shall be in proportion to the percentage of the work completed and inspected and approved by the city in no event shall the letter of credit or security instrument be reduced below the cost to complete plus ten percent 10% or $1000000 whichever is greater no more than three 3 reductions will be considered by the board of commissioners no reduction in the amount of a security instrument may be considered until after the asphalt surface binder is applied to the entire subdivision c extension of performance agreement the board of commissioners upon proof of extenuating circumstances by the applicant may extend the completion date set forth in a performance agreement and may require an increase in the amount of security to cover increases in costs d refer to planning commission the city manager will refer decisions to release reduce or extend a performance agreement to the board of commissioners e certificates of occupancy no certificate of occupancy temporary conditional or otherwise shall be issued for improvements upon any lot within a subdivision until all public improvements for said subdivision or section thereof have been fully completed dedicated and accepted by the city except for the top coat of paving which top coat may remain uninstalled but shall remain secured by the letter of credit of other security instrument 57 maintenance of improvements the applicant will be required to maintain all improvements including all lot improvements until acceptance of such public improvements by the city 58 maintenance surety upon substantial completion following substantial completion of the public improvements within a subdivision the developer will deliver to the city a dedication agreement in form and substance reasonably acceptable to the city attorney dedicating the improvements to the city and representing and warranting that all improvements have been constructed in a good and workmanlike manner commensurate with professional industry standards for similar work within the city and in accordance with all applicable plans specifications laws and regulations the developer will also deliver to the city a oneyear maintenance letter of credit in an amount of not less than fifteen percent 15% of the total cost of the improvements or as otherwise set by the board of commissioners upon the recommendation by the city manager and city engineer if during the one year following acceptance by the city of the public improvements the city determines that the public improvements have failed or require maintenance and the developer fails to promptly repair or perform maintenance the city may call upon the maintenance letter of credit in order to fund the repairs related to such failure or deficiency together with the citys administrative costs and other professionals expenses incurred in connection with the said failure or deficiency 59 expiration of agreements and letters of credit should the performance agreement lapse or expire for any reason prior to completion of all required improvements
